India

Indian (‘indhiyan) n. An American Indian (Cali-besteyn). Indiana (,indhi’yaana) gobol ku yaal bartamaha bariga US. caasimadda gobolka Indianapolis. -Indianan & adj. Indianapolis (,indhiya’naapalas) caasimadda gobolka In diana.
